Stop Payments : Costco There is a $15.00 stop payment fee. Let the member know we are sending them an email with confirmation of the temporary stop payment and under a seperate email from DocuSign, they will receive a form they need to sign and return within 14 business days in order to complete the stop payment request. if the form is not sent back to Patelco within 14 business days the stop payment will be reversed.
